2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 To enable CUDA support, UCX requires the CUDA Runtime library (libcudart).
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 The library can be installed with the appropriate command below:
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 * For CUDA 12, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=12
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 * For CUDA 13, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=13
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 If any of the packages you requested use CUDA then CUDA should already
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 have been installed for you.
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 before launching your MPI processes.
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2026-04-02T15:44:49Z #11 463.4 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
